- [P2] `parseTime` lost its `NaN` guard - [staffordersmobile.jsx:821](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L821) returns `h * 60 + m` without validating either number, so malformed working hours can produce invalid dates and broken filtering.  
FIX: restore numeric validation and return `null` for malformed times.

- [P2] AudioContext leak on unmount - [staffordersmobile.jsx:993](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L993) creates an `AudioContext`, but [staffordersmobile.jsx:2826](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L2826) never closes it.  
FIX: add unmount cleanup that calls `audioRef.current?.ctx?.close()` safely.

- [P2] Double `Стол` prefix regression is back - [staffordersmobile.jsx:1589](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L1589) and [staffordersmobile.jsx:2332](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L2332) prepend `Стол ` even though DB names already include it.  
FIX: route table labels through the guarded helper instead of manual concatenation.

- [P2] “My Tables” mixes table favorites and request favorites - request favorites are written into the same `favorites` array, but the modal counts and clears them as if they were all tables at [staffordersmobile.jsx:2290](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L2290) and [staffordersmobile.jsx:2343](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L2343).  
FIX: store table favorites separately or at least filter/count only `table:*` entries in the modal and clear action.

- [P2] Primary mobile actions are still under the 44 px touch target - examples include [staffordersmobile.jsx:1513](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L1513), [staffordersmobile.jsx:2234](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L2234), and several `min-h-[36px]` batch controls.  
FIX: raise all primary order/request actions to at least `min-h-[44px]` with consistent padding.

- [P2] Production debug logging remains - [staffordersmobile.jsx:2848](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L2848) still logs session-cleanup details to `console.log`.  
FIX: remove the logs or route them through controlled telemetry.

- [P3] Large dead/commented blocks are still in the source - the release-history header and commented-out legacy JSX leave multiple historical UI versions in one file.  
FIX: move history to docs and delete dead commented JSX from the component source.

+# Code Review Report: staffordersmobile.jsx
 
 ## Summary
-`staffordersmobile.jsx` still has two P0 cross-tenant risks and several P1 workflow regressions. `BUGS.md` was useful context: the accepted/done request flow and the deferred i18n debt are both documented there, and the current file has regressed the request flow while never resolving the i18n problem.
+`pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx` still contains two P0 access-scope bugs, several P1 workflow regressions, and unresolved platform-rule violations. I reviewed the current file against `StaffOrdersMobile README.md`, `BUGS.md`, and the cleanup helper that this page calls.
 
-## Confirmed Findings
+## Findings
 
-- [P0] Global session cleanup runs before any access or partner gate - `staffordersmobile.jsx:2844` calls `runSessionCleanup({ dryRun: false })` on mount for every visitor. The helper then loads all open sessions in `components/sessionCleanupJob.js:147` and updates them globally in `components/sessionCleanupJob.js:194`. A locked token, inactive link, or otherwise unauthorized visit can still expire other restaurants' sessions. FIX: only run cleanup after access is validated for the current restaurant, pass the current `partnerId` into the helper, and scope `TableSession`/`OrderStage`/`Order` queries by partner before mutating anything.
+- [P0] Global session cleanup runs before access is validated - `staffordersmobile.jsx:2844-2858` calls `runSessionCleanup({ dryRun: false })` on mount for every visitor, before `gateView` blocks invalid or unauthorized states. The helper then fetches all open sessions and updates them globally in `components/sessionCleanupJob.js:147-198`. A locked token, inactive invite, or otherwise unauthorized visit can still expire sessions belonging to other restaurants. FIX: only start cleanup after access is validated and the current restaurant is known, and scope the cleanup helper by `partnerId` before it reads or mutates sessions.
 
-- [P0] Access gating happens after broad data queries, so unauthorized users can fetch cross-restaurant data - `gateView` blocks UI only after hooks have already run (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3141`). Meanwhile `canFetch` becomes true for any logged-in user or token-mode link (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3216`), and when `partnerId` is null the page falls back to `Table.list()`, `Order.list()`, and `ServiceRequest.list()` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3236`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:3361`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:3383`). Invalid-role / no-partner states can therefore hit broad entity reads before the page says "Нет доступа". FIX: require validated access plus a non-null normalized `partnerId` before enabling queries, and remove the `*.list()` fallbacks entirely from this page.
+- [P0] Broad cross-restaurant data reads happen before partner access is confirmed - `canFetch` becomes true for any logged-in user (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3216-3219`), while the access UI check only happens later via `gateView` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3141-3208`). When `partnerId` is null, the page falls back to `Table.list()`, `Order.list()`, and `ServiceRequest.list()` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3234-3238`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:3359-3366`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:3381-3388`). Invalid-role or no-partner users can therefore hit broad entity reads before the page tells them "Нет доступа". FIX: require validated access plus a non-null `partnerId` before enabling any data queries, and remove the `*.list()` fallbacks from this page.
+
+- [P1] Shared `updateLinkMutation.isPending` can blank the token UI during unrelated writes - token-mode `gateView` treats `updateLinkMutation.isPending` as a binding state (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3163-3166`), but the same mutation object is also used for favorite-table writes and other `StaffAccessLink` updates (`staffordersmobile.jsx:2983-2987`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:3002-3005`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:3127-3131`). On a slow network, tapping a favorite can replace the whole screen with `BindingScreen`. FIX: split device binding/unbinding into a dedicated mutation or guard the screen with a separate `isBinding` flag instead of the shared mutation pending state.
+
+- [P1] Auto-bind can dead-end permanently on ordinary API errors - the bind effect sets `didBindRef.current = true` before calling `updateLinkMutation.mutate(...)` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3038-3045`), but `updateLinkMutation.onError` only handles rate limits and never resets that guard (`staffordersmobile.jsx:2952-2969`). If the bind request fails normally, token users stay in `bind_needed` state forever with no retry path. FIX: reset the bind guard on non-429 failures and show an explicit retry/error state for binding failures.
+
+- [P1] Logout still races device unbinding - `handleLogout` fires `updateLinkMutation.mutate(...)`, immediately clears local data, then redirects after 500 ms (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3126-3138`). If the server request is slow or fails, `bound_device_id` can remain on the old device and the next login will be locked out. FIX: make logout async, await the unbind request, and only redirect after the server-side state is updated or the user explicitly chooses to continue without unbinding.
 
-- [P1] Token auto-bind can dead-end on generic failures - the bind effect sets `didBindRef.current = true` before mutating (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3038-3045`), but `updateLinkMutation.onError` only handles 429s and never resets that guard on ordinary failures (`staffordersmobile.jsx:2952-2969`). Because `gateView` keeps returning `BindingScreen` while `tokenState === "bind_needed"` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3163-3166`), a transient API/network failure can leave token users stuck with no retry path. FIX: track binding state separately, reset the bind guard on non-rate-limit failures, and show an explicit retry/error state.
+- [P1] Standalone service requests still use the obsolete lifecycle and drop ownership metadata - `RequestCard` still renders `new -> in_progress -> done` labels (`staffordersmobile.jsx:1486-1488`), and the standalone request list still mutates `new ? "in_progress" : "done"` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:4210-4217`). That contradicts the current `BUGS.md` flow, where grouped table requests already use `accepted -> done` plus `assignee` / `assigned_at` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:2234`). FIX: reuse the same accepted/done request action builder for standalone requests and include `assignee` plus `assigned_at` when a waiter accepts a request.
 
-- [P1] Any pending `StaffAccessLink` mutation can incorrectly flip the whole page into `BindingScreen` - `gateView` treats `updateLinkMutation.isPending` as equivalent to "currently binding" (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3165`), but the same mutation object is also used for favorites updates (`staffordersmobile.jsx:2983-2987`) and clear-all favorites (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3002-3005`). In token mode, starring or clearing favorites can blank the page behind the binding screen until the mutation finishes. FIX: split binding/unbinding into its own mutation or gate on a dedicated `isBinding` flag instead of the shared mutation pending state.
+- [P1] Kitchen filtering leaks first-stage orders for custom stage pipelines - the kitchen-only filter checks `stage.internal_code !== 'start'` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3455-3467`) instead of reusing the existing first-stage detection logic from `getStatusConfig`. If a restaurant uses a custom first stage that is first by order but not literally `internal_code === 'start'`, kitchen users will see orders that should still be waiter-only. FIX: base the kitchen filter on `getStatusConfig(order).isFirstStage` or the first relevant sorted stage, not only on `internal_code`.
 
-- [P1] Logout still races device unbinding - `handleLogout` starts `updateLinkMutation.mutate(...)` and then immediately clears local data and redirects after 500 ms (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3126-3138`). On a slow or failed request, `bound_device_id` can remain on the old device and lock the link for the next login. FIX: make logout async, await the unbind update, handle failure explicitly, and redirect only after the server-side unbind succeeds or the user chooses to continue anyway.
+- [P1] The served section can show historical orders from previous table sessions - `servedOrders` is loaded with `Order.filter({ table: group.id, status: "served" })` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:1749-1754`). That query ignores `table_session`, so a current table card can include served orders from an earlier session on the same table. FIX: scope the served-orders query to the current `table_session` (or at minimum the current shift/session window) instead of only the table id.
 
-- [P1] Kitchen filtering leaks first-stage orders for custom stage pipelines - the kitchen filter uses only `stage.internal_code !== "start"` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3455-3467`). Elsewhere the page already supports first-stage detection by actual stage position, not only by `internal_code`, so restaurants using a custom first stage without that exact internal code will expose new orders to kitchen users. FIX: reuse `getStatusConfig(order).isFirstStage` or compare against the first relevant sorted stage instead of relying only on `internal_code`.
+- [P1] Link/user query failures are rendered as auth/access problems instead of retriable errors - `linkError` and `userError` only trigger special handling for rate limits (`staffordersmobile.jsx:2872-2893`). Ordinary fetch failures then fall through into misleading UI such as "Ссылка недействительна", "Необходимо войти", or "Нет доступа" (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3167-3203`). FIX: add explicit non-rate-limit error states with retry actions for the link and current-user queries instead of collapsing them into auth/access messages.
 
-- [P1] Standalone service requests still use the obsolete request lifecycle and drop assignee metadata - `BUGS.md:10-28` and `BUGS.md:47-50` document the move to `new -> accepted -> done`, but standalone `RequestCard` still renders `new -> in_progress -> done` labels (`staffordersmobile.jsx:1486-1488`) and the standalone list still mutates `new ? "in_progress" : "done"` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:4215`). Grouped table requests already use `accepted` plus `assignee` / `assigned_at` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:2234`). FIX: reuse the same accepted/done action builder for standalone requests and include `assignee` plus `assigned_at` on accept.
+- [P1] Order and request mutations fail silently outside 429 cases - `OrderCard` and `OrderGroupCard` optimistic mutations only rollback cache in `onError` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:1549-1562`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:1855-1870`), and `updateRequestMutation` only reacts to 429s (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3414-3423`). On normal API failures, the waiter gets no toast, no retry, and no explanation. FIX: add generic error handling for all mutation paths, surface a user-visible failure message, and provide a retry/recovery path.
 
-- [P1] Core order and request actions fail silently outside rate-limit cases - order mutations only rollback cache in `staffordersmobile.jsx:1558-1561` and `staffordersmobile.jsx:1864-1870`, while request mutations only react to 429s in `staffordersmobile.jsx:3417-3422`. On normal API failures, waiters get no toast, no retry path, and no actionable error state, so taps appear to do nothing. FIX: add generic error handling for all action mutations, surface a user-visible failure message, and provide a retry/recovery path.
+- [P1] File-wide i18n is still missing - `useI18n()` is effectively only used to translate `OrderStage.name` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:278-295`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:2740`), while the rest of the page is still hardcoded Russian text: status/type constants (`staffordersmobile.jsx:213-482`), gate screens (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3167-3203`), profile/settings copy (`staffordersmobile.jsx:2376-2611`), toasts (`staffordersmobile.jsx:2782-2795`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:3009`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:3116`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:3135`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:3994-4041`), and the main screen (`staffordersmobile.jsx:4078-4405`). FIX: move all user-facing strings, fallbacks, placeholders, and aria labels to `t('staff_orders_mobile...')` keys and pass `t` into helper factories/constants.
 
-- [P1] File-wide i18n violation - `useI18n()` is only used to translate `OrderStage.name` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:278-295`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:2740`), while almost all visible UI remains hardcoded Russian text: status/type constants (`staffordersmobile.jsx:213-349`), gate screens (`staffordersmobile.jsx:1393-1437`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:3167-3203`), profile/settings sheets (`staffordersmobile.jsx:2376-2611`), toasts (`staffordersmobile.jsx:2782-2795`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:3009`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:3116`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:3135`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:4037-4041`), and main page copy (`staffordersmobile.jsx:4078-4243`). `BUGS.md:361-365` already tracks this as an active deferred bug. FIX: move all user-facing strings, fallbacks, placeholders, and aria labels behind `t('page.section.key')`.
+- [P2] Shift cutoff never rolls forward while the page stays open - `shiftStartTime` is memoized only from `partnerData?.working_hours` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3230-3232`), then reused by order/request filters (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3399-3412`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:3427-3451`). If a waiter keeps the page open across midnight or a shift boundary, the filter window stays stale until a full reload. FIX: recompute the shift cutoff from a live clock tick or derive it inline from current time instead of memoizing it only on working-hours changes.
 
-- [P2] Shift cutoff is memoized once and never rolls forward while the page stays open - `shiftStartTime` is calculated with `useMemo` only from `partnerData?.working_hours` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3230-3232`), but that cutoff is then reused by both request and order filters (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3399-3412`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:3427-3451`). If the waiter keeps the page open across midnight or shift change, the current shift window stays stale until a full reload. FIX: recompute the shift cutoff from current time on a timer/state tick, or derive it inline from a live "now" value instead of memoizing it only on working-hours changes.
+- [P2] `parseTime` no longer guards against `NaN`, so malformed working hours can corrupt filtering - `getShiftStartTime()` parses `HH:MM` with `const [h, m] = timeStr.split(':').map(Number); return h * 60 + m;` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:821-825`). Invalid values flow into `setHours(...)` later (`staffordersmobile.jsx:849-865`), producing an invalid cutoff date and breaking the shift filter. FIX: restore a numeric guard in `parseTime` and treat malformed times as `null`, not as arithmetic input.
 
-- [P2] Double "Стол" prefix regression is back in multiple live paths - the project docs already note that DB table names already contain the prefix (`BUGS.md:112-116`), but the current file still prepends `"Стол "` in `RequestCard` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:1485`), `OrderCard` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:1590`), and `MyTablesModal` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:2332`). Users will see `Стол Стол 5` again. FIX: route every table label through the existing guarded helper pattern instead of manual string concatenation.
+- [P2] AudioContext is leaked on unmount - `createBeep()` creates a new `AudioContext` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:993-1019`), but the page never closes it after mount (`staffordersmobile.jsx:2826-2840`). Reopening this page repeatedly can leave browser audio resources hanging around. FIX: add an unmount cleanup effect that calls `audioRef.current?.ctx?.close()` safely.
 
-- [P2] "My Tables" mixes table favorites and request favorites, then clears both under a table-only label - request favorites are stored in the same `favorites` array via `toggleFavorite('request', ...)` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:1497-1499`), but `MyTablesModal` shows `favorites.length` as the table count (`staffordersmobile.jsx:2290-2291`), and `clearAllFavorites()` deletes the whole mixed array while saying "Столы очищены" (`staffordersmobile.jsx:2998-3009`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:4305-4311`). FIX: store table favorites and request favorites separately, or at minimum count/filter only `table:*` entries in the modal and keep the clear action scoped to tables.
+- [P2] Double `Стол` prefix regression is back in live UI paths - the project docs already note that DB table names already include the prefix, but the current UI still prepends `"Стол "` in `OrderCard` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:1589-1593`) and `MyTablesModal` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:2332`). Users can see labels like `Стол Стол 5` again. FIX: route table labels through the existing guarded helper pattern instead of manual string concatenation.
 
-- [P2] Primary mobile actions are still below the 44 px touch-target floor - many live waiter controls still use `min-h-[36px]` or even `h-7`, including request accept/serve buttons and per-row order actions (`staffordersmobile.jsx:616`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:635`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:648`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:671`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:686`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:1513`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:2131`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:2170`). On a phone, these are the main operational controls and remain too small for reliable one-handed use. FIX: raise all primary action controls in order/request flows to at least `min-h-[44px]` with consistent padding.
+- [P2] "My Tables" mixes table favorites and request favorites, then clears both under a table-only label - request favorites are stored in the same `favorites` array via `toggleFavorite('request', ...)` (`staffordersmobile.jsx:1497-1499`), but `MyTablesModal` shows `favorites.length` as the table count and `clearAllFavorites()` wipes the mixed array while saying "Столы очищены" (`staffordersmobile.jsx:2290-2291`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:2343-2352`, `staffordersmobile.jsx:2998-3009`). FIX: separate table favorites from request favorites, or at minimum count/filter only `table:*` entries inside the modal and its clear action.
 
-- [P2] Production debug logging remains in the page - session cleanup still writes to `console.log` in both success and error paths (`staffordersmobile.jsx:2848-2852`), and guest batch loading still writes `console.error` directly from the page (`staffordersmobile.jsx:3516`). These are primary operational controls on a phone and still fall below the 44 px touch-target floor. FIX: raise all primary action controls in the order/request flows to at least `min-h-[44px]` with consistent padding.

+- Attempt 1 failed immediately with `Access denied (os error 5)`.
 - Attempt 2 failed with the same access error.
-- Attempt 3 proved the root cause:
+- Attempt 3 proved the remaining blocker:
   - redirecting `CODEX_HOME` to a writable temp folder let the CLI start
-  - the CLI then failed to reach the Codex API because outbound socket/HTTPS access is blocked in this sandbox
+  - the CLI then failed to connect to the Codex API because outbound socket/HTTPS access is blocked in this environment
   - observed errors included WebSocket `os error 10013` and repeated HTTPS reconnect failures
 
 ## Conclusion
-The required independent CLI round could not complete in this environment. The final review therefore uses:
-- local Codex review
-- correctness reviewer
-- style reviewer
-
-No CLI approval/rejection output was produced, so there are no disputed findings from Round 1.
+No independent Codex CLI review output was produced, so there was no approve/reject round to merge back into the final report. The saved review is therefore based on the local code review only.

tokens used
354 050
- [P0] Unscoped session cleanup before access validation - [staffordersmobile.jsx:2844](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L2844) runs `runSessionCleanup()` on mount, and [sessionCleanupJob.js:147](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/components/sessionCleanupJob.js#L147) processes all open sessions globally. An unauthorized or mis-gated visit can expire sessions for other restaurants.  
FIX: start cleanup only after access is validated and a scoped `partnerId` is known; pass that scope into the cleanup helper.

- [P0] Cross-restaurant reads happen before partner access is confirmed - [staffordersmobile.jsx:3216](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L3216) enables fetching for any logged-in user, while [staffordersmobile.jsx:3236](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L3236), [staffordersmobile.jsx:3361](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L3361), and [staffordersmobile.jsx:3383](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L3383) fall back to broad `.list()` queries when `partnerId` is null.  
FIX: require validated access plus non-null `partnerId` before enabling any query; remove the `.list()` fallbacks from this page.

- [P1] Shared `updateLinkMutation.isPending` blanks the token UI - [staffordersmobile.jsx:3165](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L3165) treats any pending `StaffAccessLink` mutation as device binding, but the same mutation is also used for favorites and logout writes.  
FIX: split binding/unbinding into a dedicated mutation or gate `BindingScreen` with a separate `isBinding` flag.

- [P1] Auto-bind can dead-end after ordinary API failures - [staffordersmobile.jsx:3038](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L3038) sets `didBindRef` before mutating, and [staffordersmobile.jsx:2964](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L2964) never resets it on non-429 errors.  
FIX: reset the bind guard on non-rate-limit failures and show a retryable bind error state.

- [P1] Logout still races device unbinding - [staffordersmobile.jsx:3126](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L3126) fires `mutate()`, clears local state, and redirects 500 ms later. A slow/failing request can leave the device bound.  
FIX: make logout async, await the unbind request, and redirect only after success or explicit user confirmation.

- [P1] Standalone service requests still use the obsolete lifecycle - [staffordersmobile.jsx:1486](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L1486) and [staffordersmobile.jsx:4215](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L4215) still use `new -> in_progress -> done`, while grouped table requests already use `accepted -> done` with assignee metadata.  
FIX: reuse the grouped request flow for standalone requests and include `assignee` plus `assigned_at` on accept.

- [P1] Kitchen filtering leaks first-stage orders for custom pipelines - [staffordersmobile.jsx:3462](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L3462) hides only stages with `internal_code === 'start'`. A custom first stage can still appear in kitchen.  
FIX: filter via `getStatusConfig(order).isFirstStage` or the first relevant sorted stage, not raw `internal_code`.

- [P1] Served section can show historical orders from previous sessions - [staffordersmobile.jsx:1749](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L1749) loads served orders by `table` only, ignoring `table_session`.  
FIX: query served orders by current `table_session` or another current-session boundary.

- [P1] Link/user query failures are misrendered as auth/access problems - [staffordersmobile.jsx:2872](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L2872) and [staffordersmobile.jsx:2888](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L2888) only special-case 429s, so ordinary failures fall through to misleading screens like “invalid link” or “need to log in.”  
FIX: add explicit non-429 error states with retry actions for link and current-user queries.

- [P1] Order and request actions fail silently outside rate limits - [staffordersmobile.jsx:1558](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L1558), [staffordersmobile.jsx:1864](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L1864), and [staffordersmobile.jsx:3417](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L3417) rollback or do nothing, but never show a user-visible error.  
FIX: add generic `onError` handling with toast/error UI and a retry path for all mutation flows.

- [P1] File-wide i18n is still missing - `useI18n()` is only meaningfully used for stage-name translation, while the rest of the page remains hardcoded Russian across constants, screens, toasts, labels, and aria text.  
FIX: move all user-facing strings to `t('staff_orders_mobile...')` keys and pass `t` into helper/config builders.

- [P2] Shift cutoff never rolls forward while the page stays open - [staffordersmobile.jsx:3230](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L3230) memoizes `shiftStartTime` only from working hours, so midnight/shift-boundary changes are missed until reload.  
FIX: recompute against a live clock tick or derive shift cutoff inline from current time.

- [P2] `parseTime` lost its `NaN` guard - [staffordersmobile.jsx:821](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L821) returns `h * 60 + m` without validating either number, so malformed working hours can produce invalid dates and broken filtering.  
FIX: restore numeric validation and return `null` for malformed times.

- [P2] AudioContext leak on unmount - [staffordersmobile.jsx:993](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L993) creates an `AudioContext`, but [staffordersmobile.jsx:2826](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L2826) never closes it.  
FIX: add unmount cleanup that calls `audioRef.current?.ctx?.close()` safely.

- [P2] Double `Стол` prefix regression is back - [staffordersmobile.jsx:1589](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L1589) and [staffordersmobile.jsx:2332](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L2332) prepend `Стол ` even though DB names already include it.  
FIX: route table labels through the guarded helper instead of manual concatenation.

- [P2] “My Tables” mixes table favorites and request favorites - request favorites are written into the same `favorites` array, but the modal counts and clears them as if they were all tables at [staffordersmobile.jsx:2290](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L2290) and [staffordersmobile.jsx:2343](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L2343).  
FIX: store table favorites separately or at least filter/count only `table:*` entries in the modal and clear action.

- [P2] Primary mobile actions are still under the 44 px touch target - examples include [staffordersmobile.jsx:1513](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L1513), [staffordersmobile.jsx:2234](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L2234), and several `min-h-[36px]` batch controls.  
FIX: raise all primary order/request actions to at least `min-h-[44px]` with consistent padding.

- [P2] Production debug logging remains - [staffordersmobile.jsx:2848](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx#L2848) still logs session-cleanup details to `console.log`.  
FIX: remove the logs or route them through controlled telemetry.

- [P3] Large dead/commented blocks are still in the source - the release-history header and commented-out legacy JSX leave multiple historical UI versions in one file.  
FIX: move history to docs and delete dead commented JSX from the component source.
